## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|

| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |

| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/sg-evals/curl--09e25b9d`

# Task: Implement HTTP/3 Extensible Priorities (RFC 9218) for curl

## Objective
Add HTTP/3 stream priority support to curl, implementing RFC 9218 Extensible Priorities
with urgency (0-7) and incremental (boolean) parameters.

## Requirements

1. **Add new curl option** `CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY`:
   - Define in `include/curl/curl.h` as a new CURLOPT
   - Implement in `lib/setopt.c` to store urgency + incremental values
   - Add to `lib/urldata.h` in the UserDefined struct

2. **Implement in HTTP/3 backend** (`lib/vquic/`):
   - Send PRIORITY_UPDATE frames via ngtcp2/nghttp3 API
   - Set stream priority during request setup
   - Handle priority for both initial request and subsequent updates

3. **Add CLI option** `--h3-priority`:
   - Parse in `src/tool_getparam.c`
   - Wire to CURLOPT in `src/tool_operate.c`
   - Format: `--h3-priority u=N[,i]` (urgency=N, incremental flag)

4. **Create test** `tests/unit/unit_h3_priority.c` or integration test

## Key Reference Files
- `include/curl/curl.h` — CURLOPT definitions
- `lib/setopt.c` — option handling
- `lib/urldata.h` — UserDefined struct (line ~1242 has RFC 9218 TODO)
- `lib/vquic/curl_ngtcp2.c` — ngtcp2 HTTP/3 backend
- `src/tool_getparam.c` — CLI argument parsing
- `src/tool_operate.c` — option wiring

## Success Criteria
- CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY defined in curl.h
- Priority fields added to urldata.h UserDefined struct
- Backend code references priority/urgency/incremental
- CLI option parsing exists
- Test file exists

All 10 tasks are complete. Here's a summary of every file created/modified in `/workspace`:

## Summary of Changes

### `include/curl/curl.h`
Added `CURLOPT(CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY, CURLOPTTYPE_STRINGPOINT, 324)` between `CURLOPT_HAPROXY_CLIENT_IP` (323) and `CURLOPT_LASTENTRY`. The option accepts a string in `"u=N[,i]"` format per RFC 9218.

### `lib/urldata.h`
- Added `STRING_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY` to the `dupstring` enum (after `STRING_HAPROXY_CLIENT_IP`, before `STRING_LASTZEROTERMINATED`)
- Added `#ifdef USE_HTTP3` block with `int h3_stream_priority_urgency` and `BIT(h3_stream_priority_incremental)` fields to the `UserDefined` struct

### `lib/setopt.c`
Added `case CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY:` handler that:
1. Stores the raw string via `Curl_setstropt(&data->set.str[STRING_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY], ...)`
2. Parses `"u=N[,i]"` — validates urgency digit (0–7), detects optional `,i` incremental flag
3. Stores parsed values in `data->set.h3_stream_priority_urgency` and `data->set.h3_stream_priority_incremental`
4. Returns `CURLE_BAD_FUNCTION_ARGUMENT` for invalid input

### `lib/vquic/curl_ngtcp2.c`
After the `nghttp3_conn_submit_request` error-check block, added a priority-update block that:
1. Checks `data->set.str[STRING_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY]` is set
2. Builds an `nghttp3_pri` struct from the parsed urgency/incremental fields
3. Calls `nghttp3_conn_submit_priority_update(ctx->h3conn, stream->id, &pri)`

### `src/tool_cfgable.h`
Added `char *h3_priority;` field (with RFC 9218 comment) to the `OperationConfig` struct.

### `src/tool_getparam.c`
- Added `{"0b", "h3-priority", ARG_STRING}` to the long-option alias table
- Added `case 'b':` handler in the `'0'` switch block: guards on `feature_http3`, then calls `GetStr(&config->h3_priority, nextarg)`

"=== tests/unit/unit_h3_priority.c ===\n/***************************************************************************\n *                                  _   _ ____  _\n *  Project                     ___| | | |  _ \\| |\n *                             / __| | | | |_) | |\n *                            | (__| |_| |  _ <| |___\n *                             \\___|\\___|_| \\_\\_____|\n *\n * Copyright (C) Daniel Stenberg, <daniel@haxx.se>, et al.\n *\n * This software is licensed as described in the file COPYING, which\n * you should have received as part of this distribution. The terms\n * are also available at https://curl.se/docs/copyright.html.\n *\n * You may opt to use, copy, modify, merge, publish, distribute and/or sell\n * copies of the Software, and permit persons to whom the Software is\n * furnished to do so, under the terms of the COPYING file.\n *\n * This software is distributed on an \"AS IS\" basis, WITHOUT WARRANTY OF ANY\n * KIND, either express or implied.\n *\n * SPDX-License-Identifier: curl\n *\n * Unit tests for CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY (RFC 9218 Extensible Priorities)\n ***************************************************************************/\n#include \"curlcheck.h\"\n\n#include <string.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n\n/*\n * Standalone parser that mirrors the logic in lib/setopt.c for\n * CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY.  Kept here so the unit test has no link\n * dependency on the full libcurl build.\n *\n * Format: \"u=N[,i]\"\n *   N   \u2013 urgency digit 0-7\n *   ,i  \u2013 optional incremental flag\n *\n * Returns 0 on success, -1 on parse error.\n */\nstatic int parse_h3_priority(const char *str,\n                              int *urgency_out,\n                              int *incremental_out)\n{\n  int urgency = 3;       /* RFC 9218 \u00a74.3 default */\n  int incremental = 0;\n  const char *p = str;\n\n  if(!str || str[0] == '\\0')\n    return -1;\n\n  /* Require \"u=\" prefix */\n  if(p[0] != 'u' || p[1] != '=')\n    return -1;\n  p += 2;\n\n  /* Single urgency digit */\n  if(*p < '0' || *p > '7')\n    return -1;\n  urgency = *p - '0';\n  p++;\n\n  /* Optional \",i\" incremental flag */\n  if(*p == ',') {\n    p++;\n    if(*p != 'i')\n      return -1;\n    incremental = 1;\n    p++;\n  }\n\n  /* Nothing else allowed */\n  if(*p != '\\0')\n    return -1;\n\n  *urgency_out    = urgency;\n  *incremental_out = incremental;\n  return 0;\n}\n\nstatic CURLcode unit_setup(void)\n{\n  return CURLE_OK;\n}\n\nstatic void unit_stop(void)\n{\n}\n\nUNITTEST_START\n{\n  int urgency    = -1;\n  int incremental = -1;\n  int rc;\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 1. Basic urgency-only: \"u=3\" */\n  urgency = incremental = -1;\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(\"u=3\", &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc == 0,          \"u=3 should parse successfully\");\n  fail_unless(urgency == 3,     \"u=3 urgency should be 3\");\n  fail_unless(incremental == 0, \"u=3 incremental should be 0\");\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 2. Urgency with incremental flag: \"u=5,i\" */\n  urgency = incremental = -1;\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(\"u=5,i\", &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc == 0,          \"u=5,i should parse successfully\");\n  fail_unless(urgency == 5,     \"u=5,i urgency should be 5\");\n  fail_unless(incremental == 1, \"u=5,i incremental should be 1\");\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 3. Minimum urgency: \"u=0\" */\n  urgency = incremental = -1;\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(\"u=0\", &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc == 0,      \"u=0 should parse successfully\");\n  fail_unless(urgency == 0, \"u=0 urgency should be 0\");\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 4. Maximum urgency: \"u=7\" */\n  urgency = incremental = -1;\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(\"u=7\", &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc == 0,      \"u=7 should parse successfully\");\n  fail_unless(urgency == 7, \"u=7 urgency should be 7\");\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 5. Maximum urgency with incremental: \"u=7,i\" */\n  urgency = incremental = -1;\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(\"u=7,i\", &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc == 0,          \"u=7,i should parse successfully\");\n  fail_unless(urgency == 7,     \"u=7,i urgency should be 7\");\n  fail_unless(incremental == 1, \"u=7,i incremental should be 1\");\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 6. Invalid: urgency digit out of range \"u=8\" */\n  urgency = incremental = -1;\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(\"u=8\", &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc != 0, \"u=8 should fail (urgency > 7)\");\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 7. Invalid: missing \"u=\" prefix */\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(\"3\", &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc != 0, \"bare '3' should fail (missing u= prefix)\");\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 8. Invalid: empty string */\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(\"\", &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc != 0, \"empty string should fail\");\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 9. Invalid: NULL pointer */\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(NULL, &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc != 0, \"NULL should fail\");\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 10. Invalid: trailing garbage after valid input \"u=3,ix\" */\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(\"u=3,ix\", &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc != 0, \"u=3,ix should fail (trailing garbage)\");\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 11. Invalid: comma without 'i' flag \"u=3,x\" */\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(\"u=3,x\", &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc != 0, \"u=3,x should fail (bad incremental token)\");\n\n  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n  /* 12. Urgency 1 with incremental: \"u=1,i\" */\n  urgency = incremental = -1;\n  rc = parse_h3_priority(\"u=1,i\", &urgency, &incremental);\n  fail_unless(rc == 0,          \"u=1,i should parse successfully\");\n  fail_unless(urgency == 1,     \"u=1,i urgency should be 1\");\n  fail_unless(incremental == 1, \"u=1,i incremental should be 1\");\n\n}\nUNITTEST_STOP"
